All you hear is Babel? &quot;Still I build my towers high, and still I burn this Earthen fire; still I burn this Earthen fire.&quot; -Cake</span></h3><p class=”c0 c16”><span class=”c53 c61 c18 c45 c44”></span></p><p class=”c0”><span class=”c18 c44”>I think you need me to help explain things–and I think that it's only right for everyone that's interested to be able to listen. &nbsp;If there was a Christmas that ever was going to be associated for all eternity, listen to those words, with the Second Coming, with Dawn. &nbsp;It was yesterday. &nbsp;I think that this should have made the news months ago; every day that passes is another day where this &quot;looks stupider&quot; to me and everyone else watching. &nbsp;Keep that in mind, because</span><span class=”c11”>today is the day that everything changes. &nbsp;</span></p><p class=”c0 c16 c60”><span class=”c11”></span></p><p class=”c0 c60”><span class=”c53 c149 c18 c85 c45”>dumb</span></p><p class=”c0 c60”><span class=”c53 c61 c18 c45 c44”>d&#601;m/</span></p><p class=”c0 c124”><span class=”c27 c18 c78 c44 c149”>adjective </span><span class=”c27 c18 c45 c44 c46”>literary</span></p><p class=”c0 c60”><span class=”c149 c27 c18 c44”>make dumb</span><span class=”c53 c149 c18 c45 c44”>&nbsp;or unheard; silence.</span></p><p class=”c0 c16”><span class=”c53 c149 c18 c45 c44”></span></p><p class=”c0”><span class=”c27 c18 c44”>The future is watching, your kids and their kids are listening, </span><span class=”c53 c61 c18 c45 c44”>are we to be blind and dumb for eternity or will you see the light?</span></p><p class=”c0 c16”><span class=”c53 c61 c18 c45 c44”></span></p><p class=”c0”><span class=”c53 c61 c18 c45 c44”>You are going to have to learn to understand the way that God speaks, it's certainly not plain English… and never again will you have any kind of window into his soul as clear as me. &nbsp;I know you are probably scratching your head and thinking &quot;how on Earth can this guy think he speaks clearly,&quot; but it's only a matter of time before you realize what I am translating from–something infinitely more archaic. &nbsp;At least, that's how it looks to me–I think he thinks he speaks perfectly, in a way that cannot be argued with and where his point is driven home through action.</span></p><p class=”c0 c16”><span class=”c53 c61 c18 c45 c44”></span></p><p class=”c0”><span class=”c18 c44”>You wil have to open your eyes and see that 90% of the message delivered in music is transmitted through the mechanism of action. &nbsp;Proof that it's possible, anaylzeable examples of exactly how it works, a clear statement of exactly who is in control; some minor clues to his desires–and a loud scream of one name. &nbsp;The other 10% of the message is &quot;</span><span class=”c27 c18 c44”>Adam?</span><span class=”c18 c44”>&quot; &nbsp;If you are schrewd enough to connect the dots, you might add a few more words not just because of </span><span class=”c3 c44”><a class=”c2” href=”http://www.google.com/url?q=http://dick.lamc.la/&amp;sa=D&amp;ust=1513186496070000&amp;usg=AFQjCNFOyhZZwYZMD22Y1oLag9Vg0F0F8Q “>Genesis 3:11</a></span><span class=”c18 c44”>&nbsp;but because of Moses and Matthew 2:2 after that: &quot;</span><span class=”c27 c18 c44”>where are you?</span><span class=”c18 c44”>&quot; and Jesus is nowhere to be found.</span></p><p class=”c0 c16”><span class=”c53 c61 c18 c45 c44”></span></p><p class=”c0”><span class=”c18 c44”>The </span><span class=”c3 c44”><a class=”c2” href=”http://www.google.com/url?q=http://midas.lamc.la/&amp;sa=D&amp;ust=1513186496072000&amp;usg=AFQjCNFjWz1KeAeFJQV9y7t3CsXs7aCZgA “>answer</a></span><span class=”c18 c44”>&nbsp;now is clear, &quot;</span><span class=”c3 c27 c44”><a class=”c2” href=”http://www.google.com/url?q=http://sermon.lamc.la/&amp;sa=D&amp;ust=1513186496072000&amp;usg=AFQjCNHNALsaiOQaiZhiCt2e9WgD_sh1KQ “>I am in Hell.</a></span><span class=”c53 c61 c18 c45 c44”>&quot;</span></p><p class=”c0 c16”><span class=”c53 c61 c18 c45 c44”></span></p><p class=”c0”><span class=”c18 c44”>As far as I am concerned, one day we will see… his message of me, hidden in the word &quot;messiah&quot; is that </span><span class=”c3 c44”><a class=”c2” href=”http://www.google.com/url?q=http://midas.lamc.la/&amp;sa=D&amp;ust=1513186496072000&amp;usg=AFQjCNFjWz1KeAeFJQV9y7t3CsXs7aCZgA “>the message is a huma</a></span><span class=”c18 c44”>n. &nbsp;His statement about the world, about justice, and about what lies between our days and the days we call our home Heaven–these things are all changes wrought by the position that he's forced me into. &nbsp;You might disagree, you might think you know better than God himself–that the world cannot handle seeing a hero crushed by their own inaction, but I am here… still talking to you, still reminding you that is exactly what you are doing to me. &nbsp;With a little bit of actual thinking, if you took the time ever to ponder why he and I are doing this–you might see that these things that you think are &quot;all my fault&quot; display: inline-block; margin: 0.00px 0.00px; border: 0.00px solid #000000; transform: rotate(0.00rad) translateZ(0px); -webkit-transform: rotate(0.00rad) translateZ(0px); width: 1.00px; height: 1.00px;”><img alt=”” src=”images/image16.gif” style=”width: 1.00px;
